***бить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a> (730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*biti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*BʰeyH-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побить.html>поби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to beat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ше</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́тель</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:никогда.html>никогда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бьёт</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ученик.html>ученика́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V náše vrémja učítelʹ nikogdá ne <b>bʹjót</b> učeniká.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">In our time the teacher never beats the student.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладоши.html>ладо́ши</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>bitʹ</b> v ladóši</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to clap (palms), causing applause</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:режиссер.html>Режиссёр</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:привычка.html>привы́чку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ладоши.html>ладо́ши</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:привлечь.html>привле́чь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Režissjór iméjet privýčku <b>bitʹ v ladóši</b> štóby privléčʹ vnimánije.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The producer has the habit of clapping to attract attention.</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to chime <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a clock</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бью́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:башня.html>ба́шне</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Časý <b>bʹjut</b> na bášne.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The clock chimes on the top of the tower.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to churn</li></ol>

***биться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:биться.html>би́ться</a> (2526)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:биться.html>би́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">поби́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to fight, to struggle</li>
<li>to hit <i>(against)</i>, to knock <i>(against)</i>, to strike</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of heart</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to beat, to pulsate</li>
<li>to writhe, to toss about</li>
<li>to exercise oneself, to drudge, to toil</li>
<li>to break, to smash</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побить.html>поби́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pobítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***битюг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:битюг.html>битю́г</a> (30142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Named after Bityug river near Voronezh, ultimately from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:битюг.html>битю́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bitjúg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:битюг.html>битюга́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:битюг.html>битюги́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:битюг.html>битюго́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Beetewk <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a type of Russian heavy draft horse</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a very strong, heavily built man</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:бич.html>бич</a> (8562)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bičь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бич.html>бич</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bič</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бич.html>бича́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бич.html>бичи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бич.html>биче́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>whip, scourge</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southern_Russia" class="extiw" title="w:Southern Russia">Southern Russia</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> swipple</li></ol>

***блёкнувший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:блёкнувший.html>блёкнувший</a> (12938)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блёкнувший.html>блёкнувший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">bljóknuvšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блекнуть.html>блёкнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bljóknutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***благо.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a> (2429)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blago</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Displaced the inherited East Slavic form <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">бо́лого</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bólogo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">болого</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bologo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">бологъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bologŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bolgъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blágo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́га</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>благ</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> good, blessing, benefit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">economics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> good</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благополучие.html>благополу́чие</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blagopolúčije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добро́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dobró</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:счастье.html>сча́стье</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sčástʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blágo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>благо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blágo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> since, now that
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пользоваться.html>по́льзуйтесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чаем</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pólʹzujtesʹ slúčajem, <b>blágo</b> vy zdesʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">use the opportunity since you are here</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the more so because</li></ol>

***благоволить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благоволить.html>благоволи́ть</a> (25669)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">благоволити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagovoliti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blágo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́ля</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vólja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благоволить.html>благоволи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagovolítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблаговолить.html>соблаговоли́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to favour someone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:царица.html>цари́ца</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:благоволить.html>благоволи́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">caríca jemú <b>blagovolít</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the tsaress favours him</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or ironic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to do someone a favour by agreeing to do something (used with an infinitive)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благоволить.html>благоволи́те</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответить.html>отве́тить</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagovolíte</b> otvétitʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">do me a favour (and) answer</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соблаговолить.html>соблаговоли́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">soblagovolítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благовоние.html>благово́ние</a> (25196)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blágo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вонь.html>вонь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vonʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благовоние.html>благово́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagovónije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благовоние.html>благово́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благовоние.html>благово́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благовоние.html>благово́ний</a></b>)

***благодарённый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благодарить.html>благодарённый</a> (3127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодарить.html>благодарённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagodarjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодарить.html>благодари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagodarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***благодарить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благодарить.html>благодари́ть</a> (3127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">благодарити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagodariti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blágo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дарить.html>дари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">darítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодарить.html>благодари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagodarítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поблагодарить.html>поблагодари́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:отблагодарить.html>отблагодари́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to thank
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодарить.html>благодарю́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodarjú</b> za vnimánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(I) <b>thank</b> (you) for (your) attention</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодарный.html>благода́рный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">blagodárnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***благодарственный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благодарственный.html>благода́рственный</a> (25867)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">благодарьствьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagodarĭstvĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодарить.html>благодари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagodarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ство</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-stvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***благодаря.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благодаря.html>благодаря́</a> (2003)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодаря.html>благодаря́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagodarjá</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present adverbial imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодарить.html>благодари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagodarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодаря.html>благодаря́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagodarjá</span>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ dative case</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>thanks to, owing to, through (by means of), due to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разработать.html>разрабо́тали</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:компьютерный.html>компью́терную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:программа.html>програ́мму</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодаря.html>благодаря́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:новейший.html>нове́йшим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:технологический.html>технологи́ческим</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знание.html>зна́ниям</a>.</i></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i>My razrabótali nóvuju kompʹjútɛrnuju prográmmu <b>blagodarjá</b> novéjšim texnologíčeskim znánijam.</i></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><i>We developed a new computer program <b>owing to</b> recent technological knowledge.</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодаря.html>благодаря́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:важный.html>ва́жному</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:открытие.html>откры́тию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>ре́дких</a> артефа́ктов <a href = vnd.unilang:археолог.html>архео́логи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́гут</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изучать.html>изуча́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образ.html>о́браз</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлом</a>.</i></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i><b>Blagodarjá</b> vážnomu otkrýtiju rédkix artefáktov/artɛfáktov arxeólogi mógut izučátʹ óbraz žízni v próšlom.</i></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><i><b>Due to</b> the important discovery of rare artifacts, archaeologists can study the lifestyle in the past.</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:охотник.html>охо́тники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живу́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суровый.html>суро́вой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земле́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодаря.html>благодаря́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мудрость.html>му́дрости</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предок.html>пре́дков</a>.</i></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i>Oxótniki živút na suróvoj zemlé <b>blagodarjá</b> múdrosti svoíx prédkov.</i></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><i>Hunters live on this harsh land <b>due to</b> the wisdom of their forefathers.</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодаря.html>благодаря́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́гу</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзья́м</a>),</i></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><i><b>blagodarjá</b> mojemú drúgu (moím druzʹjám),</i></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><i><b>thanks to</b> my friend (my friends) that</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The preposition, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодаря.html>благодаря́</a></b>, has a positive connotation pertaining to the noun in question. By contrast, the preposition <b>из-за</b> has a negative connotation.
</p>

<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***благодатный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благодатный.html>благода́тный</a> (17053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">благодатьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagodatĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодать.html>благода́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagodátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодатный.html>благода́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagodátnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> full of divine grace, godsent, God-given</li>
<li>blissful, blessed, happy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодатный.html>благода́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тишина.html>тишина́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodátnaja</b> tišiná</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blessed/blissful silence</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>beneficial, godsent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодатный.html>благода́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:погода.html>пого́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodátnaja</b> pogóda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">propitious/benign weather</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодатный.html>благода́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздух.html>во́здух</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodátnyj</b> vózdux</i> ― <span class="e-translation">salubrious/healthful air</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодатный.html>благода́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodátnyj</b> doždʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">godsent/fertile rain</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>fertile
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодатный.html>благода́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земля́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodátnaja</b> zemljá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fertile soil</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодатный.html>благода́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:край.html>край</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodátnyj</b> kraj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">land of plenty</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодатный.html>благода́тная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чва</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodátnaja</b> póčva (dlja)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fertile ground (for)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:упасть.html>упа́сть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодатный.html>благода́тную</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:почва.html>по́чву</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">upástʹ na <b>blagodátnuju</b> póčvu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fall on fertile ground</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благодать.html>благода́ть</a> (11560)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодать.html>благода́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagodatĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blágo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодать.html>благода́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagodátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодать.html>благода́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодать.html>благода́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодать.html>благода́тей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>divine grace, boon, bliss <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a blessing or benefit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***благодушный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благодушный.html>благоду́шный</a> (19412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодушие.html>благоду́шие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagodúšije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодушный.html>благоду́шный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagodúšnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)благоду́шнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)благоду́шней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>good-natured, kindhearted
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодушный.html>благоду́шный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodúšnyj</b> málʹčik</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>good-natured</b> boy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодушный.html>благоду́шная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбка.html>улы́бка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodúšnaja</b> ulýbka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>good-natured</b> smile</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>in good spirits, pleased <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a person or mood</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благодушный.html>благоду́шное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:настроение.html>настрое́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagodúšnoje</b> nastrojénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>good</b> mood</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***благожелательный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благожелательный.html>благожела́тельный</a> (23759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">benevolēns</i>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>благо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:желать.html>жела́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">želátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тельный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-telʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***благой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>благой</a> (9000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">благъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Displaced the inherited East Slavic form, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bolgъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>благо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagój</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">stilted<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ecclesiastic or poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> good
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:благой.html>благи́ми</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:намерение.html>наме́рениями</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вымощенный.html>вы́мощена</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́га</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ад.html>ад</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>blagími</b> namérenijami výmoščena doróga v ad</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the road to hell is paved with <b>good</b> intentions</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***благообразный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благообразный.html>благообра́зный</a> (18394)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">благообразьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagoobrazĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blágo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:образ.html>о́браз</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óbraz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благообразный.html>благообра́зный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagoobráznyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)благообра́знее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)благообра́зней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>good-looking</li></ol>

***благополучие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благополучие.html>благополу́чие</a> (7004)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">благо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blago-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получить.html>получи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">polučítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благополучие.html>благополу́чие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagopolúčije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благополучие.html>благополу́чия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благополучие.html>благополу́чия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благополучие.html>благополу́чий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>well-being, prosperity, welfare <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">state of health, happiness and/or prosperity</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***благоприятный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:благоприятный.html>благоприя́тный</a> (6074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">благоприѧтьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagopriętĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благо.html>бла́го</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blágo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">прия́тие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prijátije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благоприятный.html>благоприя́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">blagoprijátnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>favourable, auspicious, advantageous</li></ol>
